why is is so slow

###### ChatGPT said:

Short answer: a few usual culprits â€” and we can nuke them fast.

## Likely causes (and fixes)

1. **In-app browser (QR â†’ X/FB/Telegram webview)**  
    Those mini browsers block redirects/popups.  
    **Fix:** open in a real browser (Safari/Chrome). Add a line on join.html: â€œIf this opened inside an app, tap â€¢â€¢â€¢ â†’ Open in Browser.â€
    
2. **VPN/ProtonVPN routing**  
    Exit nodes sometimes rate-limit Google/Discord.  
    **Fix:** toggle VPN off for the test, or pick a different exit (PH/SG/JP).
    
3. **Google Form settings**  
    Required fields or validation nags keep bouncing you to the top.  
    **Fix:** in the Form, double-check every question is required _once_, and only the **Email** field has â€œResponse validation â†’ Email.â€ Nothing else should have validation.
    
4. **Apps Script latency**  
    First run after edit is slow (cold start). UrlFetch to Discord/Telegram adds a second or two.  
    **Fix:** itâ€™s normal. After the first run, it heats up. Keep the code lean (we did).
    
5. **Discord webhook throttling**  
    Bursts can queue for a sec.  
    **Fix:** one message per submit (weâ€™re doing that), no embeds for now.
    
6. **Telegram bot delivery**  
    If you try true DMs before the user /starts the bot, it â€œfails silently.â€  
    **Fix:** weâ€™re posting to the broadcast channel with @mentions for now. DM mode needs the user to DM your bot first.
    
7. **Browser cache/stale HTML**  
    Old gate.html/join.html gets cached.  
    **Fix:** add ?v=3 to the URL while testing, or hard-refresh.
    

---

Good catch, Papi ğŸ’€ğŸ«¡ â€” the @BotFather token is what makes your Telegram bot actually talk to your channel. Without it, the Code.gs canâ€™t post invites or broadcasts.

Hereâ€™s how you get it:

ğŸª„ How to get your Telegram bot token
In Telegram, search for @BotFather (itâ€™s the official blue-check account).

Start a chat â†’ type /start.

Type /newbot.

BotFather will ask for a name (display name).

Then a username (must end with bot, e.g., VaultOpsBot or povertypimp_slayer_bot).

Boom â€” BotFather replies with something like:

Done! Congratulations on your new bot. 
Use this token to access the HTTP API:
1234567890:ABCdefGhIJKlmNoPQRstuVwxYZ
That long string (1234567890:ABC...) is your bot token.

Copy it â†’ paste it into your Script Properties as:

TG_BOT_TOKEN = 1234567890:ABCdefGhIJKlmNoPQRstuVwxYZ

function testBroadcast() {
  const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();
  const token = p.TG_BOT_TOKEN;
  const chatId = p.TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID;
  if (!token || !chatId) throw new Error('Missing TG_BOT_TOKEN or TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID');

  const url = 'https://api.telegram.org/bot' + encodeURIComponent(token) + '/sendMessage';
  const payload = { chat_id: chatId, text: 'VaultOps test âœ…', disable_web_page_preview: true };
  const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
    method: 'post',
    contentType: 'application/json',
    payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  });
  Logger.log(res.getResponseCode() + ' ' + res.getContentText());
}

function testBroadcast() {
  const token = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("TG_BOT_TOKEN");
  const chatId = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID");
  const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${token}/sendMessage`;

  const payload = {
    chat_id: chatId,
    text: "ğŸš€ VaultOps bridge is live and kicking âœ…"
  };

  const options = {
    method: "post",
    contentType: "application/json",
    payload: JSON.stringify(payload)
  };

  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
  Logger.log(response.getContentText());
}

Step 2 â€” Add these keys + values

function getProps() {

    TG_BOT_TOKEN: props.getProperty("TG_BOT_TOKEN"),
    TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID: props.getProperty("TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID"),
    DISCORD_WEBHOOK_URL: props.getProperty("DISCORD_WEBHOOK_URL"),
  };
}

function sendToBridge(message) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  
  // Telegram
  const tgToken = props.getProperty('TG_BOT_TOKEN');
  const tgChatId = props.getProperty('TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID');
  const tgUrl = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${tgToken}/sendMessage`;
  const tgPayload = {
    chat_id: tgChatId,
    text: message,
    parse_mode: 'HTML'
  };
  UrlFetchApp.fetch(tgUrl, {
    method: 'post',
    contentType: 'application/json',
    payload: JSON.stringify(tgPayload),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  });

  // Discord
  const discordWebhook = props.getProperty('DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK');
  if (discordWebhook) {
    const discordPayload = {
      content: message
    };
    UrlFetchApp.fetch(discordWebhook, {
      method: 'post',
      contentType: 'application/json',
      payload: JSON.stringify(discordPayload),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    });
  }
}

function sendToBridge(message) {

  // Telegram

    };
    UrlFetchApp.fetch(tgUrl, {
      method: 'post',
      contentType: 'application/json',

      muteHttpExceptions: true
    });
  }

  // Discord
  const discordWebhook = props.getProperty('DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK');

You left off perfectly â€” your sendToBridge(message) is already handling both Telegram and Discord. What we want now is to make sure the whole file is clean (no missing braces, no stray functions).

Hereâ€™s the final polished Code.gs ready to paste in whole (replaces your current one so you donâ€™t juggle fragments):

function sendToBridge(message) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  // --- Telegram ---
  const tgToken = props.getProperty('TG_BOT_TOKEN');
  const tgChatId = props.getProperty('TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID');

  if (tgToken && tgChatId) {
    const tgUrl = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${tgToken}/sendMessage`;
    const tgPayload = {
      chat_id: tgChatId,
      text: message,
      parse_mode: 'HTML'
    };

    UrlFetchApp.fetch(tgUrl, {
      method: 'post',
      contentType: 'application/json',
      payload: JSON.stringify(tgPayload),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    });
  }

  // --- Discord ---
  const discordWebhook = props.getProperty('DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK');
  if (discordWebhook) {
    const discordPayload = { content: message };

    UrlFetchApp.fetch(discordWebhook, {
      method: 'post',
      contentType: 'application/json',
      payload: JSON.stringify(discordPayload),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    });
  }
}

  sendToBridge("ğŸš¨ Test broadcast from VaultOps Bridge ğŸš¨");
}

ChatGPT said:

Thought for 7s
Heard, Papi. Youâ€™re solo and this needs to run handsâ€‘off. Hereâ€™s a tight, secure, â€œset it and forget itâ€ setup:

âœ… What this does (fully automated)
Ops alert on every form submission â†’ posts a clean summary to your Discord #ops.

Oneâ€‘click approvals â†’ when you tick Approved in the sheet, it autoâ€‘posts the invite to your Telegram channel (and to Discord Broadcast if you want).

Manual test button â†’ testBridge() blasts to both so you can sanityâ€‘check anytime.

ğŸ”§ Paste this WHOLE file into Code.gs
(It uses the properties you already set: DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK, TG_BOT_TOKEN, TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID. Optional: TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK if you want the post to include the private invite link.)

/***** CONFIG-LESS: pulls secrets from Script Properties *****/
function _props() {
  return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();
}

/***** LOW-LEVEL SENDERS *****/
function _sendDiscord(webhook, content) {
  if (!webhook) return;
  UrlFetchApp.fetch(webhook, {
    method: 'post',
    contentType: 'application/json',
    payload: JSON.stringify({ content }),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  });
}

function _sendTelegram(token, chatId, text) {
  if (!token || !chatId) return;
  const url = 'https://api.telegram.org/bot' + token + '/sendMessage';
  UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
    method: 'post',
    contentType: 'application/json',
    payload: JSON.stringify({ chat_id: chatId, text, parse_mode: 'HTML', disable_web_page_preview: true }),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  });
}

/***** DUAL BRIDGE (TG + Discord Broadcast) *****/
function sendToBridge(message) {
  const P = _props();
  _sendTelegram(P.TG_BOT_TOKEN, P.TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID, message);
  _sendDiscord(P.DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK, message);
}

/***** RENDERING *****/
function renderHtml_(nv) {
  // nv is e.namedValues: { "Question Title": ["value"] , ... }
  let rows = '';
  Object.keys(nv).forEach(k => {
    const v = Array.isArray(nv[k]) ? nv[k].join(', ') : String(nv[k] || '');
    rows += `<tr><td style="padding:4px 8px"><b>${escapeHtml_(k)}</b></td><td style="padding:4px 8px">${escapeHtml_(v)}</td></tr>`;
  });
  return (
    `<b>ğŸ“ New Vetting Submission</b>\n` +
    `<i>(auto-routed by VaultOps_Bridge)</i>\n\n` +
    `<b>Compact:</b> ${escapeHtml_(compactLine_(nv))}\n\n` +
    `<b>Details</b>\n` +
    `<pre>${escapeHtml_(JSON.stringify(nv, null, 2))}</pre>`
  );
}

// Short one-liner for #ops
function renderOpsSummary_(nv) {
  const alias = pick_(nv, ['Alias','Handle','Username','Name']);
  const role  = pick_(nv, ['Role','Position','Category']);
  const email = pick_(nv, ['Email','E-mail']);
  const tg    = pick_(nv, ['Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle','Signal','TG','Telegram handle']);
  return `ğŸ†• Vetting: ${alias || 'N/A'} Â· ${role || 'N/A'} Â· ${email || 'N/A'} Â· ${tg || 'N/A'}`;
}

function compactLine_(nv) {
  const alias = pick_(nv, ['Alias','Handle','Username','Name']);
  const role  = pick_(nv, ['Role','Position','Category']);
  const region= pick_(nv, ['Country','Region','City','Location']);
  return `${alias || 'N/A'} Â· ${role || 'N/A'} Â· ${region || 'N/A'}`;
}

function pick_(nv, keys) {
  for (const k of keys) {
    if (k in nv) {
      const val = Array.isArray(nv[k]) ? nv[k][0] : nv[k];
      if (val) return String(val);
    }
  }
  return '';
}

function escapeHtml_(s) {
  return String(s)
    .replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/'/g,'&#39;');
}

/***** EVENTS *****/
// 1) OPS alert on every submission (From spreadsheet â†’ On form submit)
function onFormSubmit(e) {
  try {
    const P = _props();
    const ops = P.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK;
    const nv  = e && e.namedValues ? e.namedValues : {};
    // send compact to #ops
    _sendDiscord(ops, renderOpsSummary_(nv));
    // optional: also mirror full to broadcast? keep ops clean by default.
    // sendToBridge(renderHtml_(nv));  // uncomment if you want full details broadcasted too
  } catch (err) {
    logErr('onFormSubmit', err);
  }
}

// 2) Approvals: when you tick the "Approved" checkbox, broadcast invite
// (This runs automatically on any edit in the sheet)
function onEdit(e) {
  try {
    const sheet = e.range.getSheet();
    const editedCol = e.range.getColumn();
    const editedRow = e.range.getRow();

    // Find the "Approved" column by header text (row 1)
    const headers = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === 'approved') + 1;
    if (!approvedCol) return;

    // Only react if the Approved column changed to TRUE
    if (editedCol !== approvedCol) return;
    const val = sheet.getRange(editedRow, approvedCol).getValue();
    if (val !== true) return;

    // Build a short approval message from the row
    const rowVals = sheet.getRange(editedRow, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const rowObj = {};
    headers.forEach((h,i)=> rowObj[String(h)] = rowVals[i]);

    const P = _props();
    const invite = P.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK ? `\n\nğŸ”— <a href="${P.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK}">Private Invite Link</a>` : '';
    const msg =
      `âœ… <b>Approved:</b> ${escapeHtml_(compactLine_(rowObj))}${invite}`;

    // Broadcast to TG + Discord broadcast
    sendToBridge(msg);
  } catch (err) {
    logErr('onEdit', err);
  }
}

/***** UTIL *****/
function logErr(where, err) {
  const P = _props();
  const text = `âŒ ${where}: ${err && err.message ? err.message : err}\n` +
               (err && err.stack ? `<pre>${escapeHtml_(err.stack)}</pre>` : '');
  // try to surface to ops
  _sendDiscord(P.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, text);
}

/***** MANUAL TEST *****/
function testBridge() {
  sendToBridge('ğŸš€ VaultOps Bridge test â€” Telegram + Discord are live.');
}
ğŸ§© Wireâ€‘up checklist (1 minute)
In Triggers (left sidebar clock):

Add Trigger â†’ onFormSubmit â†’ From spreadsheet â†’ On form submit.

(No trigger needed for onEdit, it runs automatically.)

Sheet column:

Make a column named Approved in row 1.

Set Data â†’ Data validation â†’ Checkbox on that column.

Optional secrets (Script Properties):

TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK = https://t.me/+... (if you want the approval post to include a join link).

ğŸ” Security notes (clean, mean, safe)
All secrets live in Script Properties (not in code).

Bot only has Post Messages in your channel. No admin creep.

Discord webhooks are rotated easily if leaked.

If you want, I can also add a custom menu (â€œVault Ops â†’ Approve selectedâ€) so you can approve in bulk without clicking checkboxes. But with the above, youâ€™re already 90% automated: submit â†’ ops ping; approve â†’ broadcast.

ğŸ”§ Add this config + helpers (top of Code.gs)
/*** === AUTO-VET BASELINE (EDIT ME) === ***/
const RULES = {
  requiredFields: ['Email', 'Alias / Handle', 'Role'],
  emailAllowDomains: ['proton.me','protonmail.com','gmail.com'],   // keep broad for now
  emailBlockDomains: ['mailinator.com','tempmail','10min'],
  minAnswerChars: 8,                                              // short = sus
  blocklistWords: ['scam','pump','xxx','porn','nft','casino'],    // add as you see patterns
  requireHandles: ['Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle','Signal','TG'], // at least one must be present
  countryAllow: [],   // e.g., ['Philippines','United States']  (empty = allow all)
  countryBlock: [],   // e.g., ['Russia','Nigeria']
  duplicateKeys: ['Email','Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle'],   // used to detect repeats
  autoApproveIf: (row) => {
    // Example: Role contains â€œEx-Patâ€ or â€œVeteranâ€ and email not from blocklist
    const role = (row['Role']||'').toString().toLowerCase();
    const email = (row['Email']||'').toString().toLowerCase();
    return (role.includes('ex-pat') || role.includes('expat') || role.includes('veteran')) &&
           !/mailinator|tempmail|10min/.test(email);
  },
  autoRejectIf: (row) => {
    // Example: any blocklist word in free-text answers
    const txt = Object.values(row).join(' ').toLowerCase();
    return RULES.blocklistWords.some(w => txt.includes(w));
  }
};

/*** === UTILS === ***/
function headerMap_(sheet){
  const headers = sheet.getRange(1,1,1,sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const map = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> map[String(h).trim()] = i+1);
  return {headers, map};
}
function rowObject_(sheet, rowIndex){
  const {headers,map} = headerMap_(sheet);
  const vals = sheet.getRange(rowIndex,1,1,headers.length).getValues()[0];
  const obj = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> obj[String(h)] = vals[i]);
  return {obj, headers, map};
}
function domainOf_(email){ const m = String(email||'').toLowerCase().match(/@([^>\s]+)/); return m?m[1]:''; }
ğŸ§  Auto-vet engine
function decide_(row){
  const reasons = [];
  const r = RULES;

  // Required fields
  for (const key of r.requiredFields){
    const v = (row[key]||'').toString().trim();
    if (!v) reasons.push(`Missing required: ${key}`);
  }

  // At least one handle
  const hasAnyHandle = r.requireHandles.some(k => String(row[k]||'').trim());
  if (!hasAnyHandle) reasons.push('No Telegram/Signal handle');

  // Email checks
  const email = (row['Email']||'').toString().trim();
  const dom = domainOf_(email);
  if (dom){
    if (r.emailBlockDomains.some(d => dom.includes(d))) reasons.push(`Blocked email domain: ${dom}`);
    if (r.emailAllowDomains.length && !r.emailAllowDomains.some(d => dom.endsWith(d))){
      reasons.push(`Unapproved email domain: ${dom}`);
    }
  } else {
    reasons.push('Invalid/missing email');
  }

  // Country allow/block (if you use a Country column)
  const country = (row['Country']||row['Location']||'').toString();
  if (r.countryBlock.length && r.countryBlock.includes(country)) reasons.push(`Blocked country: ${country}`);
  if (r.countryAllow.length && country && !r.countryAllow.includes(country)) reasons.push(`Not in allowlist country: ${country}`);

  // Minimal length sanity (catches â€œokâ€, â€œ.â€ spam)
  const shortAnswers = Object.values(row).filter(v => String(v||'').trim().length < r.minAnswerChars).length;
  if (shortAnswers > 3) reasons.push('Many very short answers');

  // Hard rules
  if (r.autoRejectIf(row)) reasons.push('Matched auto-reject rule');

  // Decision
  if (!reasons.length && r.autoApproveIf(row)) {
    return {decision:'APPROVE', score: 100, reasons:['Matched auto-approve rule']};
  }
  if (!reasons.length) {
    return {decision:'REVIEW', score: 70, reasons:['Clean but needs human eyes']};
  }
  // If only â€œlightâ€ reasons (e.g., unknown domain) you can still route to REVIEW
  const fatal = reasons.some(x => /blocked|invalid|missing required|auto-reject/i.test(x));
  return {decision: fatal ? 'REJECT' : 'REVIEW', score: fatal ? 0 : 50, reasons};
}
ğŸ”— Wire it into your sheet events
1) Auto-vet on submit â†’ ping #ops + set Status, optionally auto-approve
function onFormSubmit(e){
  try{
    const P = _props();  // from earlier file
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
    const lastRow = ss.getLastRow();
    const {obj, headers, map} = rowObject_(ss, lastRow);

    // Ensure Status & Approved columns exist
    if (!map['Status']) { ss.getRange(1, headers.length+1).setValue('Status'); map['Status']=headers.length+1; }
    if (!map['Approved']) { ss.getRange(1, headers.length+2).setValue('Approved'); map['Approved']=headers.length+2;
       ss.getRange(2, map['Approved'], ss.getMaxRows()-1, 1).insertCheckboxes(); }

    // Decide
    const res = decide_(obj);
    ss.getRange(lastRow, map['Status']).setValue(res.decision + (res.reasons.length? (' â€” '+res.reasons.join('; ')) : '') );

    // Auto-approve path
    if (res.decision === 'APPROVE') {
      ss.getRange(lastRow, map['Approved']).setValue(true); // triggers onEdit â†’ broadcast invite
    }

    // Ops ping summary
    const summary = `ğŸ†• Vetting: ${compactLine_(obj)}\nDecision: ${res.decision}\nReasons: ${res.reasons.join(' | ') || 'â€”'}`;
    _sendDiscord(P.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, summary);

  }catch(err){ logErr('onFormSubmit', err); }
}

function audit_(rowObj, decision, reasons){
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Audit') || ss.insertSheet('Audit');
  if (sh.getLastRow() === 0) sh.appendRow(['Timestamp','Decision','Reasons','Compact','Raw JSON']);
  sh.appendRow([new Date(), decision, reasons.join(' | '), compactLine_(rowObj), JSON.stringify(rowObj)]);
}
Then call audit_(obj, res.decision, res.reasons); inside onFormSubmit.

function menuApproveSelected(){
  const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
  const range = sh.getActiveRange();
  const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h=>String(h).trim().toLowerCase()==='approved')+1;
  if(!approvedCol){ SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('No "Approved" column.'); return; }
  const values = range.getValues();
  values.forEach((_,i)=> sh.getRange(range.getRow()+i, approvedCol).setValue(true));
}

Say less, Papi â€” hereâ€™s the exact row-monitor script you need.
When you tick Approved on any row, it updates Status and blasts the message to Telegram + Discord through your sendToBridge().

Paste this into your Code.gs (under your existing code)
/**
 * Fires automatically when you edit the sheet.
 * If the edit flipped the "Approved" checkbox to TRUE,
 * it updates Status and broadcasts via sendToBridge().
 */
function onEdit(e) {
  try {
    const sh = e.range.getSheet();
    // Optional: only react on the main form tab name (adjust if yours differs)
    // if (sh.getName() !== 'Form Responses 1') return;

    // Ignore header row edits
    if (e.range.getRow() === 1) return;

    // Find columns by header text in Row 1
    const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const findCol = (name) =>
      headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === name) + 1;

    const approvedCol = findCol('approved');
    const statusCol   = findCol('status');

    if (!approvedCol) return;                     // no Approved column = nothing to do
    if (e.range.getColumn() !== approvedCol) return; // not editing Approved col

    const isApproved = e.range.getValue() === true;
    const row = e.range.getRow();

    // Pull the whole row as an object {Header: Value}
    const values = sh.getRange(row, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const rowObj = {};
    headers.forEach((h, i) => (rowObj[String(h)] = values[i]));

    // Update Status text (create column if missing)
    if (!statusCol) {
      sh.getRange(1, headers.length + 1).setValue('Status');
    }
    const statusColumnIndex = statusCol || headers.length + 1;
    sh.getRange(row, statusColumnIndex).setValue(isApproved ? 'Approved âœ…' : 'Unapproved â›”');

    // Only broadcast when it becomes approved
    if (!isApproved) return;

    // Build a short message (edit as you like)
    const alias = pickField_(rowObj, ['Alias', 'Alias / Handle', 'Handle', 'Username', 'Name']) || 'N/A';
    const role  = pickField_(rowObj, ['Role', 'Position', 'Category']) || 'N/A';
    const region= pickField_(rowObj, ['Country', 'Region', 'City', 'Location']) || 'N/A';

    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();
    const invite = props.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK ? `\n\nğŸ”— <a href="${props.TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK}">Private Invite Link</a>` : '';

    const msg =
      `âœ… <b>Approved:</b> ${escapeHtml_(alias)} Â· ${escapeHtml_(role)} Â· ${escapeHtml_(region)}${invite}`;

    // Blast to Telegram + Discord Broadcast
    sendToBridge(msg);

  } catch (err) {
    logErr('onEdit', err); // uses your existing error helper
  }
}

/** helper to pick the first non-empty field from a list of header names */
function pickField_(obj, keys) {
  for (const k of keys) {
    if (k in obj && obj[k] !== '' && obj[k] != null) {
      const v = Array.isArray(obj[k]) ? obj[k][0] : obj[k];
      if (String(v).trim()) return String(v);
    }
  }
  return '';
}
How to use it

No trigger needed â€” onEdit(e) runs automatically.

Tick Approved on any row â†’

Status becomes â€œApproved âœ…â€

A message posts to Telegram (your channel) + Discord Broadcast

If you set TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK in Script Properties, itâ€™ll include the private invite link.

If your form tab isnâ€™t â€œForm Responses 1â€, uncomment the tab check and set the exact name.

Edit the 3 fields used in the message (Alias, Role, Country/Region/City) to match your exact headers.

ChatGPT said:
Lockedâ€”this is the last piece: a clean, conservative auto-vet that runs on each form submission, writes Status, and (when clearly good) ticks Approved to fire your broadcast. Minimal knobs, safe defaults.

What you paste (one block)
Drop this above your existing onFormSubmit (or replace your current onFormSubmit with the one below).

/***** === AUTO-VET RULES (edit to taste) === *****/
const AV_RULES = {
  required: ['Email','Alias','Alias / Handle','Role'],     // at least one of the Alias keys must exist
  requireOneOfAlias: ['Alias','Alias / Handle','Handle','Username','Name'],
  requireOneOfHandle: ['Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle','Signal','TG','Telegram handle'],
  allowEmailDomains: ['proton.me','protonmail.com','gmail.com','outlook.com','icloud.com'],
  blockEmailDomains: ['mailinator','tempmail','10min','yopmail'],
  blocklistWords: ['scam','pump','xxx','porn','nft','casino','loan shark'],
  minAnswerChars: 6,                                        // answers shorter than this count as â€œweakâ€
  // Strong positive hint:
  autoApproveIf: (row) => {
    const role = (row['Role']||'').toString().toLowerCase();
    return /expat|ex\-?pat|veteran|ofw/.test(role);
  }
};

/***** decision engine *****/
function autoVetDecide_(row){
  const reasons = [];
  const hasAny = (keys)=> keys.some(k => String(row[k]||'').trim());
  const get = k => String((Array.isArray(row[k]) ? row[k][0] : row[k]) || '').trim();

  // Required: email + some alias + some handle
  if (!hasAny(['Email'])) reasons.push('Missing: Email');
  if (!hasAny(AV_RULES.requireOneOfAlias)) reasons.push('Missing: Alias/Handle/Name');
  if (!hasAny(AV_RULES.requireOneOfHandle)) reasons.push('Missing: Telegram/Signal');

  // Email checks
  const email = get('Email').toLowerCase();
  const dom = (email.match(/@([^>\s]+)/)||[])[1] || '';
  if (!email) reasons.push('Invalid email');
  if (dom && AV_RULES.blockEmailDomains.some(d=>dom.includes(d))) reasons.push('Blocked email domain: '+dom);
  if (dom && AV_RULES.allowEmailDomains.length && !AV_RULES.allowEmailDomains.some(d=>dom.endsWith(d))) {
    reasons.push('Unapproved email domain: '+dom);
  }

  // Short-answer sanity
  const weak = Object.keys(row).reduce((n,k)=>{
    const v = get(k); return n + (v && v.length < AV_RULES.minAnswerChars ? 1 : 0);
  },0);
  if (weak > 3) reasons.push('Many very short answers');

  // Blocklist text scan
  const blob = Object.values(row).join(' ').toLowerCase();
  if (AV_RULES.blocklistWords.some(w=>blob.includes(w))) reasons.push('Matched blocklist word');

  // Decide
  if (reasons.length === 0 && AV_RULES.autoApproveIf(row)) {
    return {decision:'APPROVE', reasons:['Matched auto-approve rule']};
  }
  if (reasons.length === 0) return {decision:'REVIEW', reasons:['Clean but needs eyes']};

  const fatal = reasons.some(r=>/missing|invalid|blocked|blocklist/i.test(r));
  return {decision: fatal ? 'REJECT' : 'REVIEW', reasons};
}

/***** on submit: score, set Status, maybe tick Approved *****/
function onFormSubmit(e){
  try{
    const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSheet();
    const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
    const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const vals = sh.getRange(lastRow,1,1,headers.length).getValues()[0];
    const row = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> row[String(h)] = vals[i]);

    // Ensure columns exist
    let statusCol = headers.findIndex(h=>String(h).toLowerCase()==='status')+1;
    let approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h=>String(h).toLowerCase()==='approved')+1;
    if (!statusCol){ statusCol = headers.length+1; sh.getRange(1,statusCol).setValue('Status'); }
    if (!approvedCol){
      approvedCol = statusCol+1; sh.insertColumnAfter(statusCol);
      sh.getRange(1,approvedCol).setValue('Approved');
      sh.getRange(2,approvedCol,sh.getMaxRows()-1,1).insertCheckboxes();
    }

    // Decide & write status
    const res = autoVetDecide_(row);
    sh.getRange(lastRow, statusCol).setValue(`${res.decision}${res.reasons.length ? ' â€” '+res.reasons.join('; ') : ''}`);

    // Auto-approve: tick box (triggers your onEdit â†’ broadcast)
    if (res.decision === 'APPROVE') {
      sh.getRange(lastRow, approvedCol).setValue(true);
    }

    // Ping #ops with compact summary
    const P = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();
    const alias = pickField_(row, ['Alias','Alias / Handle','Handle','Username','Name']) || 'N/A';
    const role  = pickField_(row, ['Role','Position','Category']) || 'N/A';
    const region= pickField_(row, ['Country','Region','City','Location']) || 'N/A';
    const summary = `ğŸ†• Vetting: ${alias} Â· ${role} Â· ${region}\nDecision: ${res.decision}\nReasons: ${res.reasons.join(' | ') || 'â€”'}`;
    _sendDiscord(P.DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK, summary);

  } catch(err){
    logErr('onFormSubmit', err);
  }
}
What this does
Every submission â†’ scores it.

Writes Status with reasons.

If clearly good â†’ ticks Approved (your existing onEdit then broadcasts invite to Telegram + Discord).

Always sends a compact summary to #ops so you can eyeball it.

What you can tune (later)
allowEmailDomains / blockEmailDomains

blocklistWords

autoApproveIf (right now: expat/veteran/OFW in Role)

minAnswerChars

Submit a dummy entry (Incognito).

Look at the last row:

Status set with decision + reasons.

If APPROVE â†’ Approved checkbox auto-ticks â†’ you should see a broadcast in Telegram + Discord.

#ops gets the summary.

Youâ€™re set. When the clock hits your cutoff, you can sleep knowing the intake is auto-triaging and only pings you when needed.

1) â€œOps Viewâ€ dashboard (auto-build script)
This one-click function creates a new sheet called Ops View, adds KPIs, and places three live tables (Approved / Review / Rejected). It autodetects where your Status column is, so it wonâ€™t break if columns move.

Paste this in Code.gs and run buildOpsView() once.

function buildOpsView() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
  const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1') || ss.getActiveSheet();
  const {headers, map} = (function(){
    const sh = dataSh;
    const hs = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
    const m = {}; hs.forEach((h,i)=> m[String(h).trim()] = i+1);
    return {headers: hs, map: m};
  })();

  if (!map['Status']) throw new Error('No "Status" column found. Make sure Row 1 has a header named "Status".');

  const statusCol = map['Status'];
  const lastCol = dataSh.getLastColumn();
  const lastColA1 = columnToLetter_(lastCol);
  const statusA1  = columnToLetter_(statusCol);

  // make / reset Ops View
  const shName = 'Ops View';
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName(shName) ? ss.getSheetByName(shName) : ss.insertSheet(shName);
  sh.clear();

  // KPIs
  sh.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ Ops Dashboard');
  sh.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');
  sh.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA('Form Responses 1'!A2:A)`);
  sh.getRange('A4').setValue('Approved');
  sh.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "Approved âœ…")`);
  sh.getRange('A5').setValue('Review');
  sh.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "REVIEW*")`);
  sh.getRange('A6').setValue('Rejected');
  sh.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "REJECT*")`);

  // section headers
  sh.getRange('A8').setValue('âœ… Approved');
  sh.getRange('A20').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review');
  sh.getRange('A32').setValue('â›” Rejected');

  // table headers (mirror original)
  sh.getRange('A9').setValue('Live view (read-only)');
  sh.getRange('A21').setValue('Live view (read-only)');
  sh.getRange('A33').setValue('Live view (read-only)');

  // Live tables (FILTER)
  // Columns A:LAST; filter by Status exact text. If you use different emoji/text, edit the criteria.
  sh.getRange('A10').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('Form Responses 1'!A2:${lastColA1}, 'Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Approved âœ…")`
  );
  sh.getRange('A22').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('Form Responses 1'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "^REVIEW"))`
  );
  sh.getRange('A34').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('Form Responses 1'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('Form Responses 1'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}, "^REJECT"))`
  );

  sh.autoResizeColumns(1, 6);
  sh.setFrozenRows(1);
}

// helper: number â†’ letter (e.g., 1 -> A)
function columnToLetter_(n){ let s=""; while(n){ const m=(n-1)%26; s=String.fromCharCode(65+m)+s; n=(n-m-1)/26|0; } return s; }
What you get

KPIs (Total / Approved / Review / Rejected)

Three live tables you can filter/sort without touching the raw tab

Stays linked even if Status column moves

2) Tighten the baseline rules (domains + blocklist)
Drop this over your existing AV_RULES (keep the rest of your auto-vet code as-is):

const AV_RULES = {
  required: ['Email','Alias','Alias / Handle','Role'],
  requireOneOfAlias: ['Alias','Alias / Handle','Handle','Username','Name'],
  requireOneOfHandle: ['Telegram','Telegram/Signal handle','Signal','TG','Telegram handle'],

  // Allow broad but legit providers; includes common .ph mail. Edit to taste.
  allowEmailDomains: [
    'proton.me','protonmail.com','gmail.com','outlook.com','icloud.com','yahoo.com',
    '.ph' // allow local domains ending with .ph
  ],

  // Temp/disposable spammy services
  blockEmailDomains: [
    'mailinator','tempmail','10min','guerrillamail','yopmail','trashmail','sharklasers',
    'dispostable','getnada','maildrop','moakt','linshi','burnermail','inboxkitten'
  ],

  // Add mission-specific junk. Keep short and surgical.
  blocklistWords: [
    'scam','pump','dump','casino','porn','xxx','escort','betting','crypto giveaway',
    'loan shark','drop shipping','forex robot','airdrop farm'
  ],

  minAnswerChars: 6,

  // Strong positives â†’ fast lane
  autoApproveIf: (row) => {
    const role = (row['Role']||'').toString().toLowerCase();
    const about= (row['About']||row['Notes']||'').toString().toLowerCase();
    return (
      /expat|ex\-?pat|veteran|ofw|mission|journalist|ngo watchdog|anti\-corruption/.test(role+about)
    );
  }
};
Notes:

allowEmailDomains accepts suffix matches; keeping .ph in there lets legit local domains pass.

blockEmailDomains kills most throwaway inboxes.

blocklistWords focuses on spam schemes; add/remove as you see patterns.

3) Stress-test with sample data (optional but handy)
This adds 6 fake rows: clean, weak, and rejecty. Run once, then delete the rows when youâ€™re done.

function seedTestData() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1') || ss.getActiveSheet();
  const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const map = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> map[String(h)] = i);

  const rows = [
    { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'AtlasPH', Role:'Expat organizer', Email:'atlas@proton.me', Telegram:'@atlas', Country:'Philippines' },
    { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'Luna', Role:'Veteran', Email:'luna@gmail.com', Telegram:'@luna', Country:'United States' },
    { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'Shorty', Role:'ok', Email:'shorty@mailinator.com', Telegram:'', Country:'-' },
    { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'SpamLord', Role:'Crypto giveaway', Email:'spam@guerrillamail.com', Telegram:'@spam', Country:'-' },
    { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'GreyZone', Role:'research', Email:'grey@custom.ph', Telegram:'@grey', Country:'Philippines' },
    { Timestamp: new Date(), 'Alias / Handle':'Bare', Role:'-', Email:'bare@gmail.com', Telegram:'', Country:'-' },
  ];

  const out = rows.map(r => headers.map(h => r[h] ?? ''));
  sh.getRange(sh.getLastRow()+1, 1, out.length, headers.length).setValues(out);
}

/** Force-create or rebuild the Ops View tab and wire live tables */
function buildOpsView_HARD() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();         // be explicit
  const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1')      // change this if your tab name differs
              || ss.getActiveSheet();

  // Detect headers + Status column
  const headers = dataSh.getRange(1,1,1,dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  if (!headers || headers.length === 0) throw new Error('No headers found in row 1.');
  const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === 'status');
  if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('No "Status" column in row 1. Add a Status column first.');
  const statusColA1 = _colLetter(statusIdx + 1);
  const lastColA1   = _colLetter(dataSh.getLastColumn());

  // Create or reset the Ops View sheet
  const name = 'Ops View';
  let sh = ss.getSheetByName(name);
  if (sh) ss.deleteSheet(sh);                 // start clean
  sh = ss.insertSheet(name);

  // Title + KPIs
  sh.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ Ops Dashboard');
  sh.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');
  sh.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA('${dataSh.getName()}'!A2:A)`);
  sh.getRange('A4').setValue('Approved');
  sh.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"Approved âœ…")`);
  sh.getRange('A5').setValue('Review');
  sh.getRange('B5').setFormula(
    `=COUNTIF('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"REVIEW*")`
  );
  sh.getRange('A6').setValue('Rejected');
  sh.getRange('B6').setFormula(
    `=COUNTIF('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"REJECT*")`
  );

  // Sections
  sh.getRange('A8').setValue('âœ… Approved');
  sh.getRange('A20').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review');
  sh.getRange('A32').setValue('â›” Rejected');

  // Live tables
  sh.getRange('A10').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('${dataSh.getName()}'!A2:${lastColA1}, '${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1}="Approved âœ…")`
  );
  sh.getRange('A22').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('${dataSh.getName()}'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"^REVIEW"))`
  );
  sh.getRange('A34').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('${dataSh.getName()}'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusColA1}2:${statusColA1},"^REJECT"))`
  );

  sh.setFrozenRows(1);
  sh.autoResizeColumns(1, 8);
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  ss.toast('Ops View built âœ…', 'VaultOps', 3);
}

function _colLetter(n){ let s=''; while(n){ const m=(n-1)%26; s=String.fromCharCode(65+m)+s; n=(n-m-1)/26|0; } return s; }

function populateExisting_OpsView(){
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
  const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1') || ss.getActiveSheet();

  if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('No "Status" column in row 1.');

  sh.clear();
  sh.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ Ops Dashboard');
  sh.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');

  sh.getRange('A4').setValue('Approved');

  sh.getRange('A5').setValue('Review');
  sh.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('${dataSh.getName()}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"REVIEW*")`);

  );
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

function buildOpsView_PLUS(){
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');
  if (!dataSh) throw new Error('Missing tab: Form Responses 1');

  const headers = dataSh.getRange(1,1,1,dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase()==='status');
  if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('No "Status" header in row 1.');
  const statusA1 = _colLetter(statusIdx+1);
  const lastColA1 = _colLetter(dataSh.getLastColumn());
  const src = dataSh.getName();

  // nuke & rebuild Ops View
  const name = 'Ops View';
  let sh = ss.getSheetByName(name);
  if (sh) ss.deleteSheet(sh);
  sh = ss.insertSheet(name);

  // Title + KPIs
  sh.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ Ops Dashboard');
  sh.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');
  sh.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA('${src}'!A2:A)`);
  sh.getRange('A4').setValue('Approved');
  sh.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"Approved âœ…")`);
  sh.getRange('A5').setValue('Review');
  sh.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"REVIEW*")`);
  sh.getRange('A6').setValue('Rejected');
  sh.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"REJECT*")`);
  sh.getRange('A7').setValue('Pending (blank/Unapproved)');
  sh.getRange('B7').setFormula(
    `=COUNTIF('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"") + COUNTIF('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"Unapproved â›”")`
  );

  // Sections
  sh.getRange('A9').setValue('âœ… Approved');
  sh.getRange('A21').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review');
  sh.getRange('A33').setValue('â›” Rejected');
  sh.getRange('A45').setValue('ğŸŸ¡ Pending');

  // Live tables
  sh.getRange('A10').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('${src}'!A2:${lastColA1}, '${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Approved âœ…")`
  );
  sh.getRange('A22').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('${src}'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"^REVIEW"))`
  );
  sh.getRange('A34').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('${src}'!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"^REJECT"))`
  );
  // Pending = blank OR explicitly "Unapproved â›”"
  sh.getRange('A46').setFormula(
    `=FILTER('${src}'!A2:${lastColA1}, (LEN('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1})=0) + ('${src}'!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Unapproved â›”"))`
  );

  sh.setFrozenRows(1);
  sh.autoResizeColumns(1, 10);
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  ss.toast('Ops View built âœ…', 'VaultOps', 3);
}

function _colLetter(n){ let s=''; while(n){ const m=(n-1)%26; s=String.fromCharCode(65+m)+s; n=(n-m-1)/26|0; } return s; }

HAHA letâ€™s gooo, Papi! ğŸ”¥ You just spun up the Ops View like a true MFWIC Bichote. That screenshot is exactly what I expected on first boot â€” a couple quirks weâ€™ll smooth out:

#N/A under the tables = totally normal when there are no matching rows yet. Weâ€™ll wrap with IFERROR so it shows blank instead of scary text.

â€œPending (blank/Unapproved) = 100â€ = Google is counting all the empty rows in the column. Weâ€™ll switch the KPI to count only rows that actually have a Timestamp (i.e., real submissions).

Iâ€™ll patch both in one shot. Paste this, run fixOpsView() once. It will overwrite just the KPI + table formulas with the safer versions.

function fixOpsView() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');
  const ops = ss.getSheetByName('Ops View');
  if (!dataSh || !ops) throw new Error('Need "Form Responses 1" and "Ops View" tabs.');

  const headers = dataSh.getRange(1,1,1,dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase()==='status');
  if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('Add a "Status" header in row 1 first.');
  const statusA1 = _colLetter(statusIdx+1);
  const lastColA1 = _colLetter(dataSh.getLastColumn());
  const src = dataSh.getName();

  // KPIs (count only rows with a Timestamp in col A)
  ops.getRange('A3').setValue('Total Submissions');
  ops.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA(${src}!A2:A)`);
  ops.getRange('A4').setValue('Approved');
  ops.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"Approved âœ…")`);
  ops.getRange('A5').setValue('Review');
  ops.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REVIEW*")`);
  ops.getRange('A6').setValue('Rejected');
  ops.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REJECT*")`);

  // Pending = Total âˆ’ (Approved + Review + Rejected)
  ops.getRange('A7').setValue('Pending (blank/Unapproved)');
  ops.getRange('B7').setFormula(`=B3 - B4 - B5 - B6`);

  // Tables with IFERROR (show blank instead of #N/A)
  ops.getRange('A10').setFormula(
    `=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:${lastColA1}, ${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Approved âœ…"),"")`
  );
  ops.getRange('A22').setFormula(
    `=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"^REVIEW")),"")`
  );
  ops.getRange('A34').setFormula(
    `=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:${lastColA1}, REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1},"^REJECT")),"")`
  );
  ops.getRange('A46').setFormula(
    `=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:${lastColA1}, (LEN(${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1})=0) * (LEN(${src}!A2:A)>0) + (${src}!${statusA1}2:${statusA1}="Unapproved â›”")),"")`
  );

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
}

function _colLetter(n){ let s=''; while(n){ const m=(n-1)%26; s=String.fromCharCode(65+m)+s; n=(n-m-1)/26|0; } return s; }

ğŸ”¥ Full Replace Script

function buildOpsDashboard() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dataSh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');
  if (!dataSh) throw new Error('Need a tab called "Form Responses 1".');

  // Create / reset Ops Dashboard
  let ops = ss.getSheetByName('Ops Dashboard');
  if (!ops) {
    ops = ss.insertSheet('Ops Dashboard');
  } else {
    ops.clear();
  }

  // Identify Status column
  const headers = dataSh.getRange(1, 1, 1, dataSh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const statusIdx = headers.findIndex(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase() === 'status');
  if (statusIdx < 0) throw new Error('Add a "Status" header in Form Responses 1 first.');
  const statusCol = String.fromCharCode(65 + statusIdx); // Convert idx â†’ letter
  const src = `'Form Responses 1'`;

  // Title
  ops.getRange('A1').setValue('ğŸ“Š Ops Dashboard').setFontWeight("bold");

  // KPI labels
  const labels = ['Total Submissions','Approved','Review','Rejected','Pending (blank/Unapproved)'];
  ops.getRange('A3:A7').setValues(labels.map(l => [l]));

  // KPI formulas
  ops.getRange('B3').setFormula(`=COUNTA(${src}!A2:A)`);
  ops.getRange('B4').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"Approved âœ…")`);
  ops.getRange('B5').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REVIEW*")`);
  ops.getRange('B6').setFormula(`=COUNTIF(FILTER(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},LEN(${src}!A2:A)),"REJECT*")`);
  ops.getRange('B7').setFormula(`=B3-B4-B5-B6`);

  // Section tables
  ops.getRange('A9').setValue('âœ… Approved').setFontWeight("bold");
  ops.getRange('A10').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol}="Approved âœ…"),"")`);

  ops.getRange('A21').setValue('ğŸŸ£ Review').setFontWeight("bold");
  ops.getRange('A22').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},"^REVIEW")),"")`);

  ops.getRange('A33').setValue('â›” Rejected').setFontWeight("bold");
  ops.getRange('A34').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,REGEXMATCH(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol},"^REJECT")),"")`);

  ops.getRange('A45').setValue('â³ Pending').setFontWeight("bold");
  ops.getRange('A46').setFormula(`=IFERROR(FILTER(${src}!A2:ZZ,(LEN(${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol})=0)*(LEN(${src}!A2:A)>0) + (${src}!${statusCol}2:${statusCol}="Unapproved â›”")),"")`);

  ops.autoResizeColumns(1, 5);
}

Thought for 10s
Locked in. Hereâ€™s a single, drop-in script that makes the Approved checkbox drive the Status column automatically:

âœ… If the checkbox is checked â†’ Status = "Approved âœ…"

âŒ If unchecked â†’ Status = "Unapproved â›”" (or blankâ€”toggle in the code)

Runs instantly via onEdit (no trigger to add)

Includes a backfill command to sync all existing rows once

Paste this at the bottom of your Apps Script project and save.

/** Sync Status when the Approved checkbox is toggled */
function onEdit(e) {
  try {
    const sh = e.range.getSheet();
    if (!sh || sh.getName() !== 'Form Responses 1') return;     // only on the responses sheet
    const row = e.range.getRow();
    if (row < 2) return;                                        // ignore header row

    // Find column indexes by header names (robust to column moves)
    const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(h => String(h).trim());
    const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase() === 'approved') + 1;
    const statusCol   = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase() === 'status') + 1;
    if (!approvedCol || !statusCol) return;                     // required headers missing

    // Only react when the edit is in the Approved column
    if (e.range.getColumn() !== approvedCol) return;

    const checked = e.value === 'TRUE';                         // checkbox values: TRUE / FALSE
    const newStatus = checked ? 'Approved âœ…' : 'Unapproved â›”'; // change right side if you prefer "" for blank

    sh.getRange(row, statusCol).setValue(newStatus);

    // OPTIONAL: if you want to broadcast when approved, you can call your bridge here:
    // if (checked) sendToBridge(buildMessageFromRow_(sh, headers, row));
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('onEdit error:', err);
  }
}

/** One-time backfill: sync Status for every existing row based on the Approved checkbox */
function backfillApprovedToStatus() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');
  if (!sh) throw new Error('Missing "Form Responses 1" sheet.');

  const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(h => String(h).trim());
  const approvedCol = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase()==='approved') + 1;
  const statusCol   = headers.findIndex(h => h.toLowerCase()==='status') + 1;
  if (!approvedCol || !statusCol) throw new Error('Need "Approved" and "Status" headers in row 1.');

  const approvedVals = sh.getRange(2, approvedCol, lastRow-1, 1).getValues();
  const out = approvedVals.map(r => (r[0] === true ? ['Approved âœ…'] : ['Unapproved â›”'])); // or [''] if you want blank
  sh.getRange(2, statusCol, lastRow-1, 1).setValues(out);
}

/* --- OPTIONAL helper if you want to broadcast on approval --- */
// function buildMessageFromRow_(sh, headers, row){
//   const vals = sh.getRange(row, 1, 1, headers.length).getValues()[0];
//   const obj = {}; headers.forEach((h,i)=> obj[h] = vals[i]);
//   // tailor the fields you want in the message:
//   return `âœ… Approved: ${obj['Alias / Handle'] || obj['Alias'] || ''} â€¢ Email: ${obj['Email'] || ''}`;
// }

In the sheet, tick/untick any Approved checkbox â†’ watch Status update instantly.

To sync old rows: in Apps Script, run backfillApprovedToStatus() once.

1) Drop-in Control Panel (Apps Script Web App)

A) Add this server code to Code.gs (or a new file admin.gs)
function doGet() {
  return HtmlService.createTemplateFromFile('Admin')
    .evaluate()
    .setTitle('VaultOps Control Panel')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
}

// ---- secure getters/setters ----
function getStatus() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActive();
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName('Form Responses 1');
  if (!sh) throw new Error('Missing "Form Responses 1"');
  const last = sh.getLastRow();
  const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0].map(String);
  const statusCol = headers.findIndex(h => h.trim().toLowerCase()==='status')+1;
  const tsCount = sh.getRange(2,1,Math.max(0,last-1),1).getValues().filter(r=>r[0]).length;
  const statuses = statusCol ? sh.getRange(2,statusCol,Math.max(0,last-1),1).getValues().map(r=>String(r[0]||'')) : [];
  const sum = s => statuses.filter(v=>v.toUpperCase().startsWith(s)).length;
  return {
    total: tsCount,
    approved: statuses.filter(v=>v==='Approved âœ…').length,
    review: sum('REVIEW'),
    rejected: sum('REJECT'),
    pending: tsCount - (statuses.filter(v=>v==='Approved âœ…').length + sum('REVIEW') + sum('REJECT'))
  };
}

function getSettings() {
  const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const keys = [
    'DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK',
    'DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK',
    'TG_BOT_TOKEN',
    'TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID',
    'TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK'
  ];
  const out = {};
  keys.forEach(k => out[k] = p.getProperty(k) || '');
  return out;
}

function saveSettings(kv) {
  const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  Object.keys(kv||{}).forEach(k => p.setProperty(k, kv[k]));
  return true;
}

// ---- actions ----
function actionBackfill() { backfillApprovedToStatus(); return true; }
function actionBuildOps() { buildOpsDashboard(); return true; }
function actionSeed(n){ seedTestData(n||5); return true; }
function actionPurge(){ purgeSeedData_(); return true; }

// ---- optional: simple test pings ----
function pingDiscord(kind, msg){
  const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const url = p.getProperty(kind==='ops' ? 'DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK' : 'DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK');
  if (!url) throw new Error('Missing Discord webhook');
  UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {method:'post', contentType:'application/json', payload: JSON.stringify({content: msg||'VaultOps test âœ…'})});
  return true;
}
function pingTelegram(msg){
  const p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const token = p.getProperty('TG_BOT_TOKEN');
  const chatId = p.getProperty('TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID');
  if (!token || !chatId) throw new Error('Missing TG token/chat');
  const url = `https://api.telegram.org/bot${token}/sendMessage`;
  const payload = {chat_id: chatId, text: msg||'VaultOps test âœ…', parse_mode:'HTML'};
  UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {method:'post', contentType:'application/json', payload: JSON.stringify(payload), muteHttpExceptions:true});
  return true;
}
This assumes you already have backfillApprovedToStatus() and buildOpsDashboard() from earlier. If not, keep the on-edit + backfill function we added; the dashboard builder is optional.

<script>
function refresh(){
  google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(s=>{
    id('k_total').textContent = s.total;
    id('k_appr').textContent  = s.approved;
    id('k_rev').textContent   = s.review;
    id('k_rej').textContent   = s.rejected;
    id('k_pen').textContent   = s.pending;
  }).getStatus();
  google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(set=>{
    ['DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK','DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK','TG_BOT_TOKEN','TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID','TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK']
      .forEach(k=> id(k).value = set[k] || '');
  }).getSettings();
}
function save(){
  const kv = {};
  ['DISCORD_OPS_WEBHOOK','DISCORD_BROADCAST_WEBHOOK','TG_BOT_TOKEN','TG_BROADCAST_CHAT_ID','TG_GROUP_INVITE_LINK']
   .forEach(k=> kv[k] = id(k).value.trim());
  google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(()=>alert('Saved âœ…')).saveSettings(kv);
}
function run(fn){ google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(refresh)[fn](); }
function seed(){ const n = 5; google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(refresh).actionSeed(n); }
function testDiscord(kind){ google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(()=>alert('Pinged âœ…')).pingDiscord(kind==='ops'?'ops':'broadcast','VaultOps test âœ…'); }
function testTelegram(){ google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(()=>alert('Sent âœ…')).pingTelegram('VaultOps test âœ…'); }
function id(x){return document.getElementById(x);}
refresh();
</script>
</body>

  <div class="box">
    <h1>Taking you to the formâ€¦</h1>
    <p>If it doesnâ€™t open, click the button below.</p>
    <p><a id="fallback" class="btn" href="#" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Open form</a></p>
  </div>

  <script>
    // Map your forms here
    const FORMS = {
      en: "https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSd09UgirO0Gk5jlpQNJL-P3MN8FX-Bq-4VUB9XZb0J8ptAYhA/viewform",
      es: "https://docs.google.com/forms/d/REPLACE_ES_ID/viewform",
      tl: "https://docs.google.com/forms/d/REPLACE_TL_ID/viewform"
    };
    const q = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
    const lang = (q.get('lang')||'en').toLowerCase();
    const url = FORMS[lang] || FORMS.en;
    document.getElementById('fallback').href = url;
    // redirect fast
    location.replace(url);
  </script>

  <!-- In-app webview guard (optional but helpful) -->
  <script>
  (function(){
    var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
    var inApp = /(fb_iab|fbav|instagram|line|wechat|snapchat|pinterest|twitter)/.test(ua);
    if(inApp){
      document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin',
        '<div style="position:fixed;inset:0;background:#000a;color:#fff;display:grid;place-items:center;z-index:9999">'+
          '<div style="max-width:560px;background:#12141a;border:1px solid #222;border-radius:12px;padding:18px">'+
            '<b>Open in your browser</b><div style="opacity:.8;margin-top:6px">Tap â€¢â€¢â€¢ â†’ <i>Open in Browser</i> (Safari/Chrome). In-app browsers are buggy.</div>'+
          '</div></div>');
    }
  })();
  </script>
</body>

        <button onclick="unlock()">Unlock</button>
      </div>

      <div class="row" id="locked">
        <!-- Request access routes -->
        <a class="btn ghost" href="join_v2.html?lang=en&utm_source=qr&utm_medium=beta_gate&utm_campaign=vault_beta&v=2">Request Access (EN)</a>
        <a class="btn ghost" href="join_v2.html?lang=es&utm_source=qr&utm_medium=beta_gate&utm_campaign=vault_beta&v=2">Solicitar acceso (ES)</a>
        <a class="btn ghost" href="join_v2.html?lang=tl&utm_source=qr&utm_medium=beta_gate&utm_campaign=vault_beta&v=2">Humiling ng access (TL)</a>

        <!-- TODO: replace with your real Discord invite -->

      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

  <script>
    // Simple client-side code gate (keeps tourists out; not security)
    const BETA_CODE = "VAULT-777"; // <-- set your code
    const q = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
    if (q.get('code')) document.getElementById('code').value = q.get('code');

    function unlock(){
      const v = (document.getElementById('code').value || '').trim();
      const ok = v && v.toUpperCase() === BETA_CODE;
      document.getElementById('locked').style.display = ok ? 'none' : '';
      document.getElementById('unlocked').style.display = ok ? '' : 'none';
      if (!ok) alert('Invalid code. Ask an admin.');
    }
  </script>
</body>

<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
  <meta charset="utf-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1">
  <title>The Vault â€” QR Pack (Beta)</title>
  <meta name="robots" content="noindex,nofollow">
  <style>
    body{font:14px system-ui,-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,sans-serif;margin:16px}
    h1{font-size:20px;margin:0 0 12px}
    .grid{display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(2,1fr);gap:18px}
    .card{border:1px solid #ddd;border-radius:12px;padding:12px}
    .qr{width:100%;aspect-ratio:1/1;display:grid;place-items:center}
    .url{font-size:12px;word-break:break-all;color:#333}
    @media print{
      body{margin:0}
      .card{break-inside:avoid}
      .url{color:#000}
    }
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>The Vault â€” QR Pack (Beta)</h1>
  <div class="grid" id="grid"></div>

  <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/qrcodejs/1.0.0/qrcode.min.js" integrity="sha512-hX0v3GkT6gCBn+Aq1YF9XkGwm5n3J2YFJ5LwF9h5t3mKpT1J8h0m8w6m2nQx4o7c1g8E6a0+cb0Q2R6GdsVZ4w==" crossorigin="anonymous" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></script>
  <script>
    // EDIT THESE TARGETS
    const base = 'https://papiricanpi.github.io';
    const targets = [
      {label:'Discord (Beta Gate)', url: base + '/gate_beta.html?v=1'},
      {label:'Request Access â€” EN', url: base + '/join_v2.html?lang=en&utm_source=qr&utm_medium=flyer&utm_campaign=vault_beta&v=2'},
      {label:'Solicitar acceso â€” ES', url: base + '/join_v2.html?lang=es&utm_source=qr&utm_medium=flyer&utm_campaign=vault_beta&v=2'},
      {label:'Humiling ng access â€” TL', url: base + '/join_v2.html?lang=tl&utm_source=qr&utm_medium=flyer&utm_campaign=vault_beta&v=2'},
    ];

    const grid = document.getElementById('grid');
    targets.forEach(t => {
      const card = document.createElement('div');
      card.className = 'card';
      card.innerHTML = `<div style="font-weight:700;margin-bottom:8px">${t.label}</div>
                        <div class="qr" id="qr_${btoa(t.label).replace(/=/g,'')}"></div>
                        <div class="url">${t.url}</div>`;
      grid.appendChild(card);
      new QRCode(card.querySelector('.qr'), { text: t.url, width: 512, height: 512, correctLevel: QRCode.CorrectLevel.M });
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>

ğŸ’¯ Youâ€™re right â€” when we first scoped your Vault Gate, the idea was an animated intro (glitch/fade-in logo). What youâ€™ve got now (static logo only) happened because:

Security call â†’ any extra animation libraries (like external JS/CDNs) = risk of telemetry leaks, which we agreed to avoid.

If the gate pulled from an outside CDN, Cloudflare, or Google Fonts, thatâ€™s a tracking hole.

Stability for rollout â†’ a static image guaranteed the site wouldnâ€™t break while we tested Discord + gate code flow.

âœ… Options Now

Pure CSS Glitch/Fade Animation

Local JS (contained)

Runs only from GitHub Pages (no CDN).

SVG Animation

1) Drop this CSS in each pageâ€™s <head> (right before </head>)
<style>
  /* ===== Logo wrapper ===== */
  .vault-logo-wrap{
    position:relative;
    display:inline-block;
    line-height:0;
    /* adjust width only; height auto keeps it sharp on mobile */
    width:min(420px, 85vw);
    filter: drop-shadow(0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.45));
    border-radius:14px;
    overflow:hidden;
  }
  .vault-logo{
    width:100%;
    height:auto;
    display:block;
    opacity:0;                 /* start hidden, fade in below */
    animation: fadeIn .9s ease-out forwards, pulse 4s ease-in-out 1.8s infinite;
  }

  /* ===== Shiny sweep (the jig, lol) ===== */
  .shine{
    pointer-events:none;
    position:absolute; inset:0;
    background: linear-gradient(115deg,
      transparent 0%,
      rgba(255,255,255,.08) 45%,
      rgba(255,255,255,.35) 50%,
      rgba(255,255,255,.08) 55%,
      transparent 100%);
    transform: translateX(-120%);
    animation: sweep 2.4s ease-out .9s forwards, sweep 6s linear 4.2s infinite;
    mix-blend-mode: screen;
  }

  /* ===== Handle overlay ===== */
  .handle{
    position:absolute; left:0; right:0; bottom:8px;
    text-align:center;
    font:600 16px/1 system-ui,-apple-system,Segoe UI,Roboto,Inter,sans-serif;
    color:#f0e7d6; letter-spacing:.6px;
    text-shadow:
      0 1px 0 rgba(0,0,0,.35),
      0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.55);
    user-select:text;
  }

  /* ===== Optional glitch effect (add .glitch to .vault-logo-wrap) ===== */
  .glitch { filter: none; }
  .glitch .vault-logo { animation: fadeIn .9s ease-out forwards; }
  .glitch::before,
  .glitch::after{
    content:"";
    position:absolute; inset:0;
    background: url('logo.png') center/100% auto no-repeat;
    opacity:.12; mix-blend-mode:screen;
  }
  .glitch::before{ animation: g1 2.2s steps(12) infinite; transform: translate(0,0); }
  .glitch::after{  animation: g2 1.9s steps(14) infinite; transform: translate(0,0); }

  /* ===== Keyframes ===== */
  @keyframes fadeIn{
    to{opacity:1; transform:none}
    0%{opacity:0; transform: translateY(6px) scale(1.01)}
  }
  @keyframes pulse{
    0%,100%{ transform: scale(1)}
    50%{ transform: scale(1.012)}
  }
  @keyframes sweep{
    0%{ transform: translateX(-130%) rotate(0.001deg) }
    100%{ transform: translateX(130%) rotate(0.001deg) }
  }
  @keyframes g1{
    0%{ clip-path: inset(0 0 88% 0); transform: translate(-2px, -1px) }
    20%{ clip-path: inset(20% 0 60% 0); transform: translate(2px, 0) }
    40%{ clip-path: inset(40% 0 40% 0); transform: translate(-1px, 1px) }
    60%{ clip-path: inset(60% 0 20% 0); transform: translate(1px, -1px) }
    80%{ clip-path: inset(80% 0 0 0); transform: translate(-2px, 1px) }
    100%{ clip-path: inset(0 0 88% 0); transform: translate(0,0) }
  }
  @keyframes g2{
    0%{ clip-path: inset(10% 0 70% 0); transform: translate(2px,0) }
    25%{ clip-path: inset(35% 0 45% 0); transform: translate(-1px,1px) }
    50%{ clip-path: inset(55% 0 25% 0); transform: translate(1px,-1px) }
    75%{ clip-path: inset(75% 0 5% 0);  transform: translate(-2px,0) }
    100%{ clip-path: inset(10% 0 70% 0); transform: translate(0,0) }
  }
</style>

<script>
  (function(){
    const k='vault_glitch_seen';
    const wrap=document.getElementById('vaultLogo');
    if(!wrap) return;
    if(!sessionStorage.getItem(k)){
      wrap.classList.add('glitch');
      setTimeout(()=>{ wrap.classList.remove('glitch'); sessionStorage.setItem(k,'1'); }, 5000);
    }
  })();
</script>

    .vault-logo-wrap {
      position: relative;
      display: inline-block;
      line-height: 0;
      width: min(420px, 85vw);

    }

  </style>

      width:min(420px,85vw); margin:40px auto; text-align:center;

If youâ€™re okay with â€œbit.ly/your-slugâ€ showing, use this for now (and Iâ€™ll give you a QR export if you want).

Option B (best free â€œcloakingâ€): Cloudflare Worker proxy
This hides GitHub Pages completely behind a free workers.dev subdomainâ€”e.g.
povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/gate â†’ silently proxies papiricanpi.github.io/gate.html

What you get
A clean URL you can hand out (and put in QR codes).

GitHub never appears in the address bar.

Later, if you ever buy a cheap domain, you can put it behind Cloudflare and keep the same Worker.

5-minute setup
Go to dash.cloudflare.com â†’ Workers & Pages â†’ Create â†’ Worker (Free plan is fine).

Name it e.g. vault-gate.

Replace the default code with this:

// Cloudflare Worker: proxy GitHub Pages cleanly
const ORIGIN = 'https://papiricanpi.github.io';

function mapPath(pathname) {
  // nice routes -> actual files
  if (pathname === '/' || pathname === '/gate') return '/gate.html';
  if (pathname === '/join') return '/join.html';
  if (pathname === '/home') return '/home.html';
  return pathname; // pass-through for assets, etc.
}

export default {
  async fetch(request, env, ctx) {
    const url = new URL(request.url);
    url.host = new URL(ORIGIN).host;
    url.protocol = 'https:';
    url.pathname = mapPath(url.pathname);

    // Proxy the request to GitHub Pages
    const init = {
      method: request.method,
      headers: request.headers,
      body: ['GET','HEAD'].includes(request.method) ? undefined : await request.arrayBuffer(),
      redirect: 'follow',
      cf: { cacheTtl: 300, cacheEverything: true },
    };

    // Forward the request
    const resp = await fetch(url.toString(), init);

    // Strip cross-origin headers that can leak the origin or block embedding
    const newHeaders = new Headers(resp.headers);
    newHeaders.delete('x-github-request-id');
    newHeaders.delete('server');
    newHeaders.set('x-proxied-by', 'workers.dev');

    return new Response(resp.body, { status: resp.status, headers: newHeaders });
  }
}
Save & Deploy.

In the Workerâ€™s â€œTriggersâ€ tab, add a Route like:

povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/* (it uses your free workers.dev subdomain)

Your new clean links (examples)
Gate: https://povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/gate

Join: https://povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/join

Home: https://povertypimpslayer.workers.dev/home

Drop those into your QR codes, Substack, Twitter, Telegram, etc. No one sees GitHub.

Option C: Free host mirror (Netlify/Vercel)
Hook your repo to Netlify or Vercel and youâ€™ll get a nicer free URL like
thevault.netlify.app or thevault.vercel.app.

Still not your brand, but â€œ*.appâ€ looks more pro than GitHub Pages.

You can also add the Cloudflare Worker in front later if you want extra privacy.

What Iâ€™d do for you right now

â€¦workers.dev/gate

â€¦workers.dev/home

Youâ€™ll see a default Worker script (something like return new Response("Hello World!")).

export default {
  async fetch(request) {
    const url = new URL(request.url);

    // Forward everything to your GitHub Pages
    const target = "https://papiricanpi.github.io";

    // Map paths
    let path = url.pathname;
    if (path === "/") path = "/gate.html"; // default landing page
    if (path.startsWith("/gate")) path = "/gate.html";
    if (path.startsWith("/join")) path = "/join.html";
    if (path.startsWith("/home")) path = "/index.html";

    return fetch(target + path, {
      method: request.method,
      headers: request.headers,
      body: request.body
    });
  }
}

https://yourworkername.username.workers.dev
